###  Toivo₁

* _This proper noun overlaps  very common *toivo* (hope)._
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  1
* Origins: [fiwikt](https://fi.wiktionary.org/wiki/Toivo) [enwikt](https://fi.wiktionary.org/wiki/Toivo) finer joukahainen 
* Possible NER class:  FIRST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
* Semantic tags:  MALE


###  Toivo₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Toivo* (hope)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  1
* Origins: [fiwikt](https://fi.wiktionary.org/wiki/Toivo) [enwikt](https://fi.wiktionary.org/wiki/Toivo) finer joukahainen 
* Possible NER class:  FIRST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
* Semantic tags:  MALE
